\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
API headers and documentation for the mmgs library. 

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Algiane Froehly (Inria/\+UBordeaux) 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxyVersion}{Version}
5 
\end{DoxyVersion}
\begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
01 2014 
\end{DoxyDate}
\begin{DoxyCopyright}{Copyright}
GNU Lesser General Public License.
\end{DoxyCopyright}
These are the API functions for the mmgs library. These functions allow to load and save meshes and data defined on meshes; add, extract, or modify mesh data; and to call the library functions that perform remeshing and level-\/set discretization.

Meshes are here defined in terms of vertices and two-\/dimensional objects\+: triangles and quadrangles, which live in 3D space. Edges can also be represented. All of these {\itshape entities} can have a {\itshape reference\+:} an integer value that can serve as a group identifier. In addition mesh entities can have {\itshape attributes} such as \char`\"{}required\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}corner\char`\"{}.

Data defined on meshes can be for example functions that are meant for level-\/set discretization and metric tensors that will govern edge lengths. These data can be scalar, vector, or (symmetric) tensor-\/valued; and there can be more than one data item associated with a mesh entity. These data are often referred to as {\itshape solutions}.

Two of the functions here are referred to as \char`\"{}programs\char`\"{}, because they perform the tasks for which mmgs is meant\+: meshing and level-\/set discretization. The other functions merely serve to load and save data and to perform pre-\/ and post-\/processing. These programs actually behave much like independent programs\+: they send diagnostic output to stdout and in rare cases they may call the exit() function. 

Definition in file \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgs_8h_source}{libmmgs.\+h}}.

Check if the numbers of given entities match with mesh and solution size and check mesh data. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the solution structure. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}
This function checks if the numbers of given entities match with the mesh and solution sizes and checks the mesh data. Use of this function is not mandatory.

\index{libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}!MMGS\_Compute\_eigenv@{MMGS\_Compute\_eigenv}}
\index{MMGS\_Compute\_eigenv@{MMGS\_Compute\_eigenv}!libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Compute\_eigenv()}{MMGS\_Compute\_eigenv()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Compute\+\_\+eigenv (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{m\mbox{[}6\mbox{]},  }\item[{double}]{lambda\mbox{[}3\mbox{]},  }\item[{double}]{vp\mbox{[}3\mbox{]}\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute the real eigenvalues and eigenvectors of a symmetric matrix. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em m} & upper part of a symmetric matrix diagonalizable in $\vert$R \\
\hline
{\em lambda} & array of eigenvalues \\
\hline
{\em vp} & array of eigenvectors\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the order of the eigenvalues
\end{DoxyReturn}
Compute the real eigenvalues and eigenvectors of a symmetric matrix m whose upper part is provided (m11, m12, m13, m22, m23, m33 in this order).

lambda\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}0,1\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}0,2\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(1,\+:) in fortran

lambda\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}1,1\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}1,2\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(2,\+:) in fortran

lambda\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}2\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}2,1\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}2,2\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(3,\+:) in fortran

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMGS\+\_\+\+COMPUTE\+\_\+\+EIGENV(m,lambda,vp,retval)~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: m($\ast$)~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: lambda($\ast$),vp($\ast$)~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Free\_all()}{MMGS\_Free\_all()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Free\+\_\+all (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const int}]{starter,  }\item[{}]{... }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Deallocations before return. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em starter} & dummy argument used to initialize the variadic argument list. \\
\hline
{\em ...} & variadic arguments.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
For the \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgs_8c_a734fba39f5d78f79b63c0a4bc2df973c}{MMGS\+\_\+mmgslib}} function, you need to call the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__s_8c_a30741f0d1b895b92e6ea43f6370b0367}{MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh}} function with the following arguments \+: MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met, \&your\+\_\+metric,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

For the \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgs_8c_a523792a545ccb3e575fc6f5d30218199}{MMGS\+\_\+mmgsls}} function, you need to call the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__s_8c_a30741f0d1b895b92e6ea43f6370b0367}{MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh}} function with the following arguments \+: MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Ls, \&your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

Here, {\itshape your\+\_\+mesh} is a \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}, {\itshape your\+\_\+metric} and {\itshape your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set} are \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 on success
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
we pass the structures by reference in order to have argument compatibility between the library call from a Fortran code and a C code.

no Fortran interface to allow variadic args. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\end{DoxyReturn}
Find the indices of the 3 adjacent elements of triangle {\itshape kel}. $v_i = 0$ if the $i^{th}$ face has no adjacent element (so we are on a boundary face).

\index{libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}!MMGS\_Get\_edge@{MMGS\_Get\_edge}}
\index{MMGS\_Get\_edge@{MMGS\_Get\_edge}!libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Get\_edge()}{MMGS\_Get\_edge()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+edge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Ridge,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices, reference, and attributes of the next edge in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em e0} & pointer to the index of the first vertex of the edge. \\
\hline
{\em e1} & pointer to the index of the second vertex of the edge. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the edge reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Ridge} & pointer to the flag saying if the edge is ridge. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if the edge is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the extremities {\itshape e0}, {\itshape e1}, reference {\itshape ref}, and attributes of the next edge of {\itshape mesh}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all edges. When it has been called as many times as there are edges in the mesh, the internal edge counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMGS\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+EDGE(mesh,e0,e1,ref,is\+Ridge,is\+Required,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+OUT)\+:: e0,e1~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: ref~\newline
 INTEGER \+:: is\+Ridge,is\+Required~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Get\_ithSol\_inSolsAtVertices()}{MMGS\_Get\_ithSol\_inSolsAtVertices()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+ith\+Sol\+\_\+in\+Sols\+At\+Vertices (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{int}]{i,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{s,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{pos }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get one out of several solutions at a specific vertex. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sol} & pointer to the array of solutions \\
\hline
{\em i} & position of the solution field that we want to get. \\
\hline
{\em s} & solution(s) at mesh vertex {\itshape pos}. The required size of this array depends on the type of solution. \\
\hline
{\em pos} & index of the vertex on which we get the solution.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retreives the value of field {\itshape i} of the solution array at vertex {\itshape pos}. ({\itshape pos} from 1 to the number of vertices included and {\itshape i} from 1 to the number of solutions). It works for any type of solution; the types are inferred from {\itshape sol}.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMGS\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+ITHSOL\+\_\+\+INSOLSATVERTICES(sol,i,s,pos,retval)~\newline

 INTEGER, INTENT(\+IN) \+:: i~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: pos~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), DIMENSION($\ast$),INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: s~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

Get one out of several solutions at all vertices in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sol} & pointer to the array of solutions \\

\hline

\end{DoxyParams}

0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the values of field {\itshape i} of the solution array {\itshape sol} ({\itshape i} from 1 to {\itshape the} number of solutions). It works for any type of solution; the type is inferred from {\itshape sol}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Get\_nonBdyEdge()}{MMGS\_Get\_nonBdyEdge()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+non\+Bdy\+Edge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{idx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get vertices and reference of a non-\/boundary edge. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em e0} & pointer to the first extremity of the edge (a vertex number). \\
\hline
{\em e1} & pointer to the second extremity of the edge (a vertex number). \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the edge reference. \\
\hline
{\em idx} & index of the non boundary edge to get (between 1 and the number of edges) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function returns the vertices {\itshape e0}, {\itshape e1} and reference {\itshape ref} of the non boundary edge {\itshape idx}. An edge is boundary if it is located at the interface of 2 domains with different references, if it belongs to one triangle only or if it is a singular edge (ridge or required).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: idx~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges()}{MMGS\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+number\+Of\+Non\+Bdy\+Edges (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{nb\+\_\+edges }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the number of non-\/boundary edges. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em the} & number of edges pointer to the number of non boundary edges. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Get the number of non-\/boundary edges (for DG methods for example). An edge is boundary if it is located at the interface of 2 domains with different references, if it belongs to one triangle only or if it is a singular edge (ridge or required). Append these edges to the list of edges.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
reallocate the edge array and append the internal edges. This may modify the behaviour of other functions.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+scalar\+Sol (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{s }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the next element of a scalar solution structure. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em met} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em s} & pointer to the scalar solution value. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the next element {\itshape s} of the solution field {\itshape met}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all elements. When it has been called as many times as there are elements in the solution, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Get\_tensorSol()}{MMGS\_Get\_tensorSol()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+tensor\+Sol (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m11,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m12,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m13,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m22,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m23,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m33 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the next element of a tensor solution structure. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em met} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em m11} & pointer to the position (1,1) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m12} & pointer to the position (1,2) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m13} & pointer to the position (1,3) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m22} & pointer to the position (2,2) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m23} & pointer to the position (2,3) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m33} & pointer to the position (3,3) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the next element $(m_{11},m_{12},m_{13},m_{22},m_{23},m_{33})$ of a tensor-\/valued solution field. It is meant to be called in a loop over all vertices. When it has been called as many times as there are elements in the solution, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMGS\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+TENSORSOL(met,m11,m12,m13,m22,m23,m33,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: met~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: m11,m12,m13,m22,m23,m33~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+triangle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices, reference, and required attribute of the next triangle in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em v0} & pointer to the first vertex of the triangle. \\
\hline

\hline

\hline

\hline

\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the vertices {\itshape v0}, {\itshape v1}, {\itshape v2}, reference {\itshape ref}, and required attribute {\itshape is\+Required} of the next triangle of {\itshape mesh}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all triangles. When it has been called as many times as there are triangles, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{libmmgs_8h_ae51595d6e021e5501ca5eae6919572e8}\label{libmmgs_8h_ae51595d6e021e5501ca5eae6919572e8}} 
\index{libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}!MMGS\_Get\_vertex@{MMGS\_Get\_vertex}}
\index{MMGS\_Get\_vertex@{MMGS\_Get\_vertex}!libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Get\_vertex()}{MMGS\_Get\_vertex()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+vertex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c0,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c1,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Corner,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the coordinates {\itshape c0}, {\itshape c1},{\itshape c2} and reference {\itshape ref} of the next vertex of {\itshape mesh}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em c0} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the first dimension. \\
\hline
{\em c1} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the second dimension. \\
\hline
{\em c2} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the third dimension. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the vertex reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Corner} & pointer to the flag saying if the vertex is corner. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if the vertex is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the coordinates {\itshape c0}, {\itshape c1},{\itshape c2}, reference {\itshape ref}, and attributes of the next vertex of a mesh. It is meant to be used in a loop over all vertices. When this function has been called as many times as there are vertices, the internal loop counter will be reset. To obtain data for a specific vertex, the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__s_8c_a81ba4da9950966c613b45f00a7cc5fe4}{MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+By\+Idx\+\_\+vertex}} function can be used instead.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMGS\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+VERTEX(mesh,c0,c1,c2,ref,is\+Corner,is\+Required,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: c0,c1,c2~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: ref~\newline
 INTEGER \+:: is\+Corner,is\+Required~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Get\_vertices()}{MMGS\_Get\_vertices()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+vertices (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{vertices,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{refs,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{are\+Corners,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{are\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the coordinates, references and attributes of all vertices in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em vertices} & pointer to the array of coordinates. The coordinates of vertex {\itshape i} are stored in vertices\mbox{[}(i-\/1)$\ast$3\mbox{]}@3. \\
\hline
{\em refs} & pointer to the array of vertex references. The ref of vertex {\itshape i} is stored in refs\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
{\em are\+Corners} & pointer to the array of flags saying if vertices are corners. are\+Corners\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]}=1 if vertex {\itshape i} is corner. \\
\hline
{\em are\+Required} & pointer to the table of flags saying if vertices are required. are\+Required\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]}=1 if vertex {\itshape i} is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: (commentated in order to allow to pass \%val(0) instead of the refs,are\+Corners and are\+Required arrays) \begin{quote}

! INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), DIMENSION($\ast$) \+:: refs~\newline
! INTEGER, DIMENSION($\ast$) \+:: are\+Corners,are\+Required~\newline

\end{quote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_GetByIdx\_vertex()}{MMGS\_GetByIdx\_vertex()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Get\+By\+Idx\+\_\+vertex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c0,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c1,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Corner,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{idx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the coordinates and reference of a specific vertex in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em c0} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the first dimension. \\
\hline
{\em c1} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the second dimension. \\
\hline
{\em c2} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the third dimension. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the vertex reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Corner} & pointer to the flag saying if the vertex is corner. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if the vertex is required. \\
\hline
{\em idx} & index of vertex to get. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the coordinates {\itshape c0}, {\itshape c1}, {\itshape c2} and reference {\itshape ref} of vertex {\itshape idx} of mesh, as well as its \char`\"{}corner\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}required\char`\"{} attributes.

\end{quote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Init\_mesh()}{MMGS\_Init\_mesh()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const int}]{starter,  }\item[{}]{... }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initialize a mesh structure and optionally the associated solution and metric structures. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em starter} & dummy argument used to initialize the variadic argument list \\
\hline
{\em ...} & variadic arguments.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
For the MMGS\+\_\+mmgslib function, you need to call the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__s_8c_a30741f0d1b895b92e6ea43f6370b0367}{MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh}} function with the following arguments \+: MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met, \&your\+\_\+metric,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

For the \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgs_8c_a523792a545ccb3e575fc6f5d30218199}{MMGS\+\_\+mmgsls}} function, you need to call the {\itshape MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh} function with the following arguments \+: MMGS\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Ls, \&your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

Here, {\itshape your\+\_\+mesh} is a \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}, {\itshape your\+\_\+metric} and {\itshape your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set} are \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 on success, 0 on failure
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
No fortran interface, to allow variadic arguments. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\index{MMGS\_loadMesh@{MMGS\_loadMesh}!libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_loadMesh()}{MMGS\_loadMesh()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+load\+Mesh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Load a mesh (in .mesh/.mesb format) from file. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & name of the file to load. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function reads .mesh (ASCII) and .meshb (binary) files. If the name contains \char`\"{}.\+mesh\char`\"{} the file will be read as an ASCII file and if the name contains .meshb it be read as a binary file. If the file contains neither of these strings the function will first try to open \char`\"{}\mbox{[}filename\mbox{]}.\+meshb\char`\"{} and if this fails it will try \char`\"{}\mbox{[}filename\mbox{]}.\+mesh\char`\"{}.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMGS\+\_\+\+LOADMESH(mesh,filename,strlen0,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T, INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 CHARACTER(LEN=$\ast$), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: filename~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+IN) \+:: strlen0~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+load\+Msh\+Mesh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Load a mesh and possibly a solution in .msh format from file. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the solution structure. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & name of the file to load. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Read a mesh and optionally one data field in MSH file format (.msh extension). We read only low-\/order vertices, edges, triangles, quadrangles, tetrahedra and prisms.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+load\+Vtu\+Mesh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Load a mesh and possibly data in VTU (VTK) format from file. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the metric structure or the NULL pointer. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the level-\/set structure or the NULL pointer. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & name of the file to load. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Read a mesh and optionally one data field in VTK vtu file format (.vtu extension). We read only low-\/order vertices, edges, triangles and quadrangles.

\index{libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}!MMGS\_saveMshMesh\_and\_allData@{MMGS\_saveMshMesh\_and\_allData}}
\index{MMGS\_saveMshMesh\_and\_allData@{MMGS\_saveMshMesh\_and\_allData}!libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_saveMshMesh\_and\_allData()}{MMGS\_saveMshMesh\_and\_allData()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+save\+Msh\+Mesh\+\_\+and\+\_\+all\+Data (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}} $\ast$}]{sol,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Save a mesh and multiple data fields in MSH format, ascii or binary depending on the filename extension. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the solution structure. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & name of the file to write. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function saves a mesh and multiple data fields (that are considered as solutions and not metrics, thus, we do nothing over the ridge vertices) in MSH file format (.msh extension). The file is saved in ASCII format for .msh extension and in binary format for a .mshb extension.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMGS\+\_\+\+SAVEMSHMESH\+\_\+\+AND\+\_\+\+ALLDATA(mesh,sol,filename,strlen0,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T, INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh,sol~\newline
 CHARACTER(LEN=$\ast$), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: filename~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+IN) \+:: strlen0~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+constant\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute a constant size map. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the sol structure \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 on success
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function computes a constant size map according to mesh-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}info.\+hsiz, mesh-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}info.\+hmin and mesh-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}info.\+hmax. It updates these 3 values if they are not compatible.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+ith\+Sol\+\_\+in\+Sols\+At\+Vertices (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{int}]{i,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{s,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{pos }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set a single element of one out of multiple solution fields that are defined on vertices. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sol} & pointer to the array of solutions \\
\hline
{\em i} & position of the solution field that we want to set. \\
\hline
{\em s} & solution(s) at mesh vertex {\itshape pos}. \\
\hline
{\em pos} & index of the vertex on which we set the solution.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Set values of the solution at field {\itshape i} of the solution array and at position \textbackslash{}pos ({\itshape pos} from 1 to the number of vertices included and {\itshape i} from 1 to the number of solutions). The type of solution is determined from {\itshape sol}.

\index{MMGS\_Set\_lsBaseReference@{MMGS\_Set\_lsBaseReference}!libmmgs.h@{libmmgs.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Set\_lsBaseReference()}{MMGS\_Set\_lsBaseReference()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+ls\+Base\+Reference (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{br }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set a new level-\/set base reference. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em br} & new level-\/set base reference. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Set a new level-\/set base reference of ref {\itshape br} in level-\/set discretization mode. Base references are boundary conditions to which an implicit domain can be attached. All implicit volumes that are not attached to listed base references are deleted as spurious volumes by the {\itshape rmc} option.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMGS\+\_\+\+SET\+\_\+\+LSBASEREFERENCE(mesh,sol,br,retval)~\newline

 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN)\+:: br~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMGS\_Set\_multiMat()}{MMGS\_Set\_multiMat()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgs__export_8h_a57be058d1a94523e9b9d5494e05be609}{LIBMMGS\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMGS\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+multi\+Mat (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ref,  }\item[{int}]{split,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{rmin,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{rplus }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the reference mapping for the elements of reference {\itshape ref} in level-\/set discretization mode. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & input triangle reference. \\
\hline
{\em split} & MMG5\+\_\+\+MMAT\+\_\+\+No\+Split if the entity must not be split, MMG5\+\_\+\+MMAT\+\_\+\+Split otherwise \\
\hline
{\em rmin} & reference for the negative side after LS discretization \\
\hline
{\em rplus} & reference for the positive side after LS discretization \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
With this function you can determine which references will be given to the triangles on both sides of the level set, after discretization. Negative and positive here refer to areas where the function is smaller or larger, respectively, than the isovalue of the level set.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
